It is very convenient to bring 2 children. There are free fruits. 2 Journey to the West comic books were also given.

The service is very good, the service staff are very friendly, take the initiative to say hello, and take the initiative to help give away the small blind box and mobile phone holder of Journey to the West before leaving. I dropped something when I got off the taxi, and I found it the next day.

The sanitary environment is good, there is a Wanda Plaza 800 to 900 meters away. It takes about 25 minutes to take a taxi to the Journey to the West and Huai'an East Station. It is very convenient to take a taxi, the car drives directly to the door, and it doesn't rain.

The breakfast is OK, but there are too many people during the May Day holiday. If you want to find a table for 4, you need to wait for a while.

msg:I went to Huai'an with my wife for two days on the weekend. The main attractions in Huai'an: the former residence of the Prime Minister, Huai'an Prefecture Office, Hexia Ancient Town, the No. 1 Scholar's Mansion, and the former residence of Wu Cheng'en are relatively concentrated, all in the southern Huai'an District. After a whole day of walking during the day, in order to take a boat to cruise the inner canal at night and experience the night view of "the canal is three thousand miles long, and the most beautiful is Huai'an", I chose the Jinling Hotel in Huaiyin District at night. This choice is undoubtedly correct. The hotel belongs to the Jinling Group, with a beautiful environment, complete facilities, clean and hygienic, especially considerate service, which reflects the heritage of a five-star hotel everywhere. Special thanks to the front desk staff for arranging a very quiet room. The bed and pillow are very comfortable, allowing me, a person with sleep disorders, to sleep all night. It is really good, and I will choose the Jinling brand in the future.
